In one sentence: The theme suite is a mess, I advise you to quit.
1. When I entered the room, a string of blue lights on the ceiling almost blinded my eyes. I searched for a long time but couldn't find the switch (there was no light switch near the door of the room). I searched in the dark for a long time before I found the light switch on the bedside and another wall. I made a few phone calls and the maintenance worker fiddled with it for a long time before finding that the light was broken;
2. There are so many small lights in the room. After turning off the main power switch, you have to unplug the plugs and sockets one by one to enjoy the dark sleep time. Finally, I found that there is a solar-powered light, and unplugging it doesn't work. I was so angry that I hid behind the curtains;
3. Look at the picture below, who can guess which one is the door? (The correct answer is the right side. I don't know what the door on the left is. It is locked and can't be opened. I am a little afraid that someone will come in from this door in the middle of the night);
4. It is said to be an astronomy theme suite, but the room is on the first floor. There are trees outside. I asked the room service staff how to use the telescope. They told me that the magnification is not enough and I can only see the opposite side of the lake. I used the telescope as a magnifying glass to see the trees? (The telescope also has three cracks);
5. I don't know who designed this suite. I can't figure it out without a cerebral thrombosis for thousands of years. The three separations are realized, but no one should like to be watched when taking a bath or going to the toilet;
6. Since it is a children's theme suite, it is not called a children's suite just by putting two picture books, two building blocks and hanging a planet lamp. The corresponding facilities are not kept up at all, such as the washbasin does not have a two-step stair bench and no children's pillows are provided;
7. The buffet restaurant looks bright in the photo, but it is very dim in reality. I think it would not be a good mood to have breakfast in such an environment. There is also a problem with the placement of the buffet. The fruits are placed away from the main group and in the farthest corner.
All the stars in the rating are given to the waiters. The overall service is OK.

msg:The biggest selling point is the location of the hotel. The appearance is also very design-oriented. The petal island of Dishui Lake and the surrounding environment are refreshing.
I stayed there when it was still a Crown Hotel a few years ago. The overall feeling was okay at that time, but the single dining options were disappointing.
Now it has been upgraded to InterContinental. After the renovation, the hardware has been improved, and the dining options have become more. Members are provided with welcome drinks when they come to the store. The happy hour in the executive lounge is also rich. The hot and cold meals and drinks are enough for me to make a simple meal. The breakfast room is large and the meals are distributed more scattered. The advantage is that it avoids dense gatherings to pick up meals, but it also brings the inconvenience of going around the restaurant to choose meals. The food options and tastes are quite satisfactory, and the cheese is quite rich!
The room has a good view, facing the outdoor swimming pool and Dishui Lake, and the bedding is moderately soft and hard. But the TV is very stuck. After playing the hotel welcome video, other functions are basically in a dead state; the hotel is newly renovated but not equipped with automatic bathroom.
The service a**osphere of the hotel staff still has a lot of room for improvement. Except for the checkout guy who showed a friendly and polite attitude, other staff did not take the initiative to greet or smile. They basically ignored or even avoided them. This is still not in line with the service standards of InterContinental.
The overall feeling is acceptable, but it is not a highly favored InterContinental.

msg:InterContinental Shanghai Dishui Lake is a beautiful petal-shaped hotel located on Dishui Hunan Island, in the center of Dishui Lake. A unique accommodation experience for your first stay. It can be said that where the river flows into the East China Sea, you can enjoy the tranquility of lakes, islands and tranquility.
In front of the hotel, the clear waves of the welcoming stream are rippling and singing, and a colorful building stands in the stream. The hotel's address "Nantao No. 1" is eye-catching and unique. Feel: the reflection of the big lake in the distance and the creek nearby.
The hotel environment is a harmonious combination of European and American style and ancient Chinese architecture.
During the day, the hotel has luxuriant trees and deep winding paths outdoors; the ancient courtyards are well-proportioned; the lakeside walkway offers a panoramic view of the beautiful scenery far and near, making you feel relaxed and happy; at night, the night view is bright and quiet and beautiful. The sunrise in winter is brilliant and colorful; the fog is shrouded, making it feel like a fairyland on earth. The open-air infinity swimming pool, relying on the blue sky and clear water, is endlessly relaxing.
The guest rooms are luxurious and elegant, and the service is exquisite; the breakfast is rich in variety; and there are ample parking spaces in the basement.
Manager Ye Ting of Caifenglou Restaurant takes the lead in taking time out from her busy schedule to take the initiative to receive suggestions; her professionalism and exquisiteness are similar to Japanese style. Supervisor Yao Zongxian is attentive and courteous to guests; foreman Yao Shenghui is proactive, enthusiastic, patient and kind; intern Chen Xinyue is proactive and responsive.
Lu You, the foreman at the front desk, was polite and caring; Qian Hongyu, the front office clerk, was professional, skilled, conscientious and meticulous, and took the trouble to arrange for express mailing.
The head of the concierge depar**ent, Zhao Yisen, is proactive and enthusiastic and answers all questions; Li Rui is gentle and approachable in every possible way.
Shang Qiyong, the waiter on the 3rd floor of Area D, adheres to professional standards for cleaning rooms, is proactive and hardworking, and greets politely.

Above, I am deeply impressed and will never leave. First choice for staying again.

It enjoys the beautiful scenery of Dishui Lake and has a private island of 75,000 square meters. It integrates the beautiful image of "Peach Blossom Spring" into the space design. It creates a quiet place away from the hustle and bustle of the city and becomes an ideal destination for city vacations, family outings, business meetings, romantic weddings and private events. Luxurious rooms and suites The hotel is hidden under five graceful "petals", allowing you to enjoy the beautiful scenery of the lake and Lingang New City from multiple dimensions. The oversized luxurious and comfortable living experience enjoys exclusive privacy among modern aesthetics, fashion art and technological trends. Rooms start from 45 square meters in size and are spacious and transparent. 80% of the rooms are equipped with cruise ship-style viewing balconies and spacious seating areas. The bathrooms are equipped with oversized viewing bathtubs, where guests can soak in the bathtub to relieve the fatigue of the day. Enjoy the beautiful outdoor scenery. The suite area ranges from 85 square meters to 114 square meters to meet your different needs for leisure, office and party. The rooms designed on the cruise ship terrace echo the lake view, making you feel like you are traveling on the sea. InterContinental Executive Club The InterContinental Executive Club is located on the 3rd floor of Area C. It is cleverly divided into upper and lower floors by a spiral staircase. It is a private space for business discussions, gatherings and leisure.
